<review>Los Cocos is a true treasure of east bay restaurants and El Salvadorian food.  The food is hand-made before your eyes. The papusas are $2.70 for two.  You can't go wrong with any of choices--from the spinach, to the beans to the cheese and chicharr√≥n.  They come with a wonderful vinegary 'slaw' and homemade hot sauce.  The papusa travel well if you are planning on taking them home for dinner or a party.  The El Salvadorian tamales ($3 each) are soft, fluffy and I don't know what they are filled with except that it's wonderful. Be warned: they always have at least one olive (with the pit!) in them.  The chile rellenos, the carne asada, the platanos con crema, and soups are all excellent. The black beans at Los Cocos are outstanding.  Equally impressive is the Casamiento (rice mixed with onions and black beans) which is clearly the El Salvadorian version of Peruvian tacu-tacu.  The casamiento rice dish is so delicious it's hard to describe. The ladies who cook and serve are delightfully kind and helpful.  The restaurant is clean, warm and welcoming and there is street parking outside and around the block in this safe neighborhood.  If you are looking for great, tasty food and a fun experience, Los Cocos is the place to go.</review>< UserId.>

<rating>1<//rating>< Text>
I sometimes take my wife and my two daughters here to have pupusas, but today is our last time we go here.  I wasn't quite hungry today but the rest of my family was, so I ordered one pupusa each for my kids and two for my wife and one for me.  The one for me was the problem, apparently adults have to order a minimum of two, which isn't stated in the menu very clearly.  What is stated is that there is a minimum order of two pupusas, and since we ordered a total of five I thought we were in the good; I was wrong!  Instead I had my wife order 3 pupusas, one that I will eat.  The waitress brought out 3 sets of utensils and 3 plates, and refused service to me.  This is just bad business and I wished this was the only thing that went wrong but it wasn't.  To add to the bad service, my wife ordered a can of coconut water and it came to her filthy.  She couldn't even get it totally cleaned with the napkin she received, so she returned it for a different bottled drink which was much easier too clean.  And to nail the coffin shut, one of the male employee's came from the rear of the restaurant, which is where the restroom is located, he was adjusting his parts.  Granted that he was doing this above his pants but still, that isn't ok, I don't care who you are.</Text>

<Review>This place is beautifully decorated, employs a wonderful staff, and is lead by an incredibly knowledgeable doctor. As I walked into their office, the team warmly welcomed me into their cozy practice. The front office staff guided me through signing in and filling out the necessary paper work. They called me back within 15 minutes of signing in.

As a first time eye patient, the doctor's assistant made the initial examination enjoyable. Once completed, Dr. Fenema conducted a few more examinations to determine my exact prescription. He also educated me on the different parts of the eye and explained any details pertaining to my situation. The initial eye examination took about an hour to complete.

<Pictures>None< /Pictures><rate>5< /rate><user_id>100037122105550812864< /user_id><Review>TL;DR I recommend Mr. Khalid from UIF. Thank you to UIF for providing this service. Follow the steps mentioned in the review to make the process easier and quicker.

We worked with Mr. Khalid from UIF, he is helpful, hard working and prompt. As a first time buyer, I had so many questions. He went above and beyond to answer our questions and explain the steps, he was prompt to reply and take actions. He even replied our questions during weekend. He is professional and he knows a lot, I learned a lot from him as a first time buyer. Thank you for your hard work and being so patient with us. We appreciate it.

Everything is explained well just before starting the process with UIF. Their partnership program does not have LLC fee and there is no prepayment penalty. UIF portal was straightforward and easy to understand. Uploading documents and e-signing the documents were smooth experience. It is good to have such service for people who are conscious about interests. I want to say thanks to UIF for providing such service for us.

Since I had to learn with try and error and I want to suggest followings to people who plan to buy property:
1. Talk to UIF (or whichever company you plan to use) about requirements then decide property type (single or multi family) and decide if it will be primary residence or investment property.
2. Get pre-qualified before starting property research since it will make finding a good value property and negotiating easier
3. Find a good real estate agent and ask if you will have to pay any fees or commission as a buyer (normally, buyers don't pay fees or commissions to real estate agents). be careful, some agents request some kind of fee from buyer up to $500.
4. Talk to UIF just before writing offer for the property to make sure you are writing the offer you can afford according to current policies
5. After agreement with seller, communicate regularly with UIF, real estate agent, escrow and seller to make sure you can close in a month. Ask always, if they are waiting anything from you. Arrange your closing date close to end of the month to pay less daily profit rate.
5. Make sure to get final closing disclosure 3 work days before closing date. This way, you would not have to rush in closing date.

Sorry for long review.<//Review><gmap_id>0x808fec76105b5fab:0x67ff355b209b860f<//gmap_id><resp>None< /resp><Name>homer simpson</Name><Date>1606287086903</Date></record></dataset><record>
